<p>Det är lika stor sannolikhet över hela intervallet <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>a</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">[a,b]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit">a</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathit">b</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span>. Sannolikheten är därför <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>P</mi><mo>(</mo><mi>a</mi><mo>≤</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>≤</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mrow><mi>b</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>a</mi></mrow></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P(a \le X \le b) = \frac{1}{b-a}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; <p><em>Exponentialfördelning</em> <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>X</mi><mo>∈</mo><mtext>Exp</mtext><mo>(</mo><mi>λ</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\quad X \in \text{Exp}(\lambda)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.72243em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Exp</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">λ</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>X</mi></msub><mo>(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">{</mo><mtable><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mn>0</mn></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>≤</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>λ</mi><msup><mi>e</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mi>λ</mi><mi>x</mi></mrow></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>&amp;gt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">f_X(x) = \begin{cases} 0 &amp;amp; <p><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>F</mi><mi>X</mi></msub><mo>(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">{</mo><mtable><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mn>0</mn></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>&amp;lt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>e</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mi>λ</mi><mi>x</mi></mrow></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>≥</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">F_X(x) = \begin{cases} 0 &amp;amp; <p><em>-Bevis-</em><br>
Enligt definitionen för fördelningsfunktionen:<br>

<p><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mo>∫</mo><mn>0</mn><mi>x</mi></msubsup><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>X</mi></msub><mo>(</mo><mi>t</mi><mo>)</mo><mi>d</mi><mi>t</mi><mo>=</mo><msubsup><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><msub><mi>F</mi><mi>X</mi></msub><mo>(</mo><mi>t</mi><mo>)</mo><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow><mn>0</mn><mi>x</mi></msubsup><mo>=</mo><mo>[</mo><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>e</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mi>λ</mi><mi>t</mi></mrow></msup><msubsup><mo>]</mo><mn>0</mn><mi>x</mi></msubsup><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>e</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mi>λ</mi><mi>x</mi></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>e</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mi>λ</mi><mn>0</mn></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>e</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mi>λ</mi><mi>x</mi></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><mo>(</mo><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>e</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mi>λ</mi><mi>x</mi></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\int_0^x f_X(t)dt = \left [ F_X(t)\right]_0^x = [-e^{-\lambda t}]_0^x = -e^{-\lambda x} - -e^{-\lambda 0} = -e^{-\lambda x} - (-1) = 1 -e^{-\lambda x}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.21511em; <p><em>Normalfördelning</em> <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>X</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>N</mi><mo>(</mo><mi>μ</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>σ</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\quad X \in N(\mu,\sigma)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.72243em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">N</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">μ</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">σ</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>X</mi></msub><mo>(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mrow><mi>σ</mi><msqrt><mrow><mn>2</mn><mi>π</mi></mrow></msqrt></mrow></mfrac><msup><mi>e</mi><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>μ</mi><msup><mo>)</mo><mn>2</mn></msup><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mn>2</mn><msup><mi>σ</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mo>−</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∞</mi><mo>&amp;lt;</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>&amp;lt;</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∞</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">f_X(x) = \frac{1}{\sigma \sqrt{2\pi}}e^{(x-\mu)^2/2\sigma^2},\quad -\infty &amp;lt; <p><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>σ</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\sigma</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">σ</span></span></span></span></span> kallas standardavvikelsen (kommer senare).</p>
<h2 id="flertvådimensionella-stokastiska-variabler">Fler(/Två)dimensionella stokastiska variabler</h2>
<p>Notation: <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>Y</mi><mo>)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo>(</mo><mi>Z</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>W</mi><mo>)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(X,Y),(Z,W),</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">Z</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">W</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mpunct">,</span></span></span></span></span> osv.<br>
En stokastisk variabel är en funktion som definerar ett talpart<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>(</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>y</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(x_i,y_i)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; <h3 id="det-diskreta-fallet-1">Det <em>diskreta</em> fallet</h3>
<p><strong>Sannolikhetsfunktionen</strong><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>p</mi><mrow><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>Y</mi></mrow></msub><mo>(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>P</mi><mo>(</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>j</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>Y</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>k</mi><mo>)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>j</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>k</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>1</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>2</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo>…</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">p_{X,Y}(x,y) =P(X = j, Y = k), \quad j,k= 0,1,2,\dots</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; <p><em>Marginella sannolikhetsfunktionen</em><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>X</mi></msub><mo>(</mo><mi>j</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><msubsup><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∞</mi></msubsup><msub><mi>P</mi><mrow><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>Y</mi></mrow></msub><mo>(</mo><mi>j</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>k</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">p_X(j) = \sum_{k=0}^\infty P_{X,Y}(j,k)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; <p><strong>Fördelningsfunktionen</strong><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>Y</mi></mrow></msub><mo>(</mo><mi>j</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>k</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>P</mi><mo>(</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>≤</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>Y</mi><mo>≤</mo><mi>y</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><msub><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>j</mi><mo>≤</mo><mi>x</mi></mrow></msub><msub><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo>≤</mo><mi>y</mi></mrow></msub><msub><mi>p</mi><mrow><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>Y</mi></mrow></msub><mo>(</mo><mi>j</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>k</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">F_{X,Y}(j,k) = P(X \le x, Y \le y) = \sum_{j \le x} \sum_{k \le y} p_{X,Y}(j,k)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span><span class="mrel mtight">≤</span><span class="mord mathit mtight">x</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.435818em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mop op-symbol small-op" style="position: relative; <h3 id="det-kontinuerliga-fallet-1">Det <em>kontinuerliga</em> fallet</h3>
<p><strong>Täthetsfunktionen</strong><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>f</mi><mrow><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>Y</mi></mrow></msub><mo>(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">f_{X,Y}(x,y)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathit">A</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.16082em; vertical-align: -0.35582em;"></span><span class="mop op-symbol small-op" style="margin-right: 0.19445em; position: relative; top: -0.00056em;">∫</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mop op-symbol small-op" style="margin-right: 0.19445em; position: relative; top: -0.00056em;">∫</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.122511em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.34418em; margin-left: -0.19445em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">A</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.35582em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; <p><strong>Fördelningsfunktionen</strong><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>Y</mi></mrow></msub><mo>(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>P</mi><mo>(</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>≤</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>Y</mi><mo>≤</mo><mi>y</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>P</mi><mo>(</mo><mo>−</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∞</mi><mo>&amp;lt;</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>≤</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo>−</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∞</mi><mo>&amp;lt;</mo><mi>Y</mi><mo>≤</mo><mi>y</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">F_{X,Y}(x,y) = P(X \le x, Y \le y) = P(-\infty &amp;lt; <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>=</mo><msubsup><mo>∫</mo><mrow><mo>−</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∞</mi></mrow><mi>y</mi></msubsup><msubsup><mo>∫</mo><mrow><mo>−</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∞</mi></mrow><mi>x</mi></msubsup><msub><mi>f</mi><mrow><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>Y</mi></mrow></msub><mo>(</mo><mi>u</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>v</mi><mo>)</mo><mi>d</mi><mi>u</mi><mi>d</mi><mi>v</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">=\int_{-\infty}^y \int_{-\infty}^xf_{X,Y}(u,v)dudv</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.36687em; margin-left: -0.19445em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">−</span><span class="mord mtight">∞</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.2579em; <p>Fördelningsfunktionen beskriver summeringen av den förbrukade sannolikheten till och med värdet/punkten <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(x,y)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">x</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<h2 id="väntevärde">Väntevärde</h2>
<p>Det för<strong>vänt</strong>ade genomsnittliga värdet över ett oändligt antal försök.</p>
<p><strong>Det diskreta fallet</strong><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>E</mi><mo>(</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><msub><mo>∑</mo><mi>k</mi></msub><mi>k</mi><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>X</mi></msub><mo>(</mo><mi>k</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">E(X) = \sum_{k} kp_X(k)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">E</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.04971em; vertical-align: -0.29971em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mop op-symbol small-op" style="position: relative; top: -5e-06em;">∑</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.186398em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.40029em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.29971em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">p</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><strong>Det kontinuerliga fallet</strong></p>
</div>
